< Review>
Costly billing mistake by staff is going to cost me $1,443.60.

I have been a patient at Bright Now Dental for about 2 years.  During the end of my 1st year, staff billed my insurance for more than what was allowed for 3 implants and assured me that it would be covered.

The bill was NOT paid by my insurance.  Bright Now Dental over the course of a year,  assured me that it was probably a coding error and they would get things worked out with my insurance.

During my last visit, the staff asked me to call my insurance about payment?  My insurance informed me Bright Now Dental billed my insurance for more than what was allowed for the year.

I spoke to staff that it was NOT a coding error.  Simply put, staff billed my insurance for more than what was allowed for the year.

I had NOT heard anything back from Bright Now Dental until today.  I received a letter from a collection agency saying I'm delinquent on my account with Bright Now Dental for $1,443.60????

So, instead of admitting to and paying for their own mistake, Bright Now Dental sent my account to collections????  Bright Now Dental did NOT even have the common courtesy to call me so that we could have the issue decided by an arbitration as agreed to in writing prior to the procedure.

Now, I have to notify the collection agency that Bright Now Dental for $1,443.60 staff billed my insurance for more than what was allowed for the year.

WHAT NEXT???

I'm NOT going back to Bright Now Dental<//Review>

< Text>
3 cavities in same arc, with standard dental insurance, the co-pay that I paid out of pocket was $175.00.
The doctor's administering the treatment are very courteous and accommodating.
The female receptionist apparently saw that I rode my motorcycle in because she made a comparison at what I was willing to spend for a motorcycle, but not what I was willing to pay for other pricey treatment. She literally asked me how much I paid for my motorcycle.
I got the impression that was a shaming tactic, directed at embarrassing me to get more dental work done.
When I was asked the doctor about how much more it would cost to repair a cavity on the left quadrant, because I needed some clarification on the prices.
The doctor's assistant called a young woman in the financial department, who walked in and stomped her Wal-Mart special high heels shoes with dominance, and said that she had went over the prices with me.
I thought she was arrogant and unnecessarily rude.
The couple times I visited the Bright Now Dental as a patient, I found that there is a lot paperwork to read and sign and date, as if you are purchasing an automobile from a dealership.
Parking is easy, the waiting area has small inexpensive chairs and tables with magazines and a small play pen area for children. It is not the most appealing at a glance-looked more like I was at DMV arbitrarion office or traffic school. The lighting in the office was dimmed than what you expect for a dental office.
The examination rooms looked clean and organize. The equipment used by the staff appears sterile, modern, and clean. I am discourage to go back.<//Text>

<user>100260747996083633407</user><name>Sue Chae< /name><Date>1525659936288<//Date><Rating>1<//Rating>< text>
My school has been fundraising for villages in Africa with very little access to clean water. Most of our students come from low-income families so we held a Penny War to collect change. In order to raise more money, some of the staff members went and bought a box of pennies ($25) from their banks to contribute to the cause. All the loose coins were exchanged for cash through Coin Star, but I wanted to deposit the rolled coins because to my knowledge rolled coins can be deposited to my account at my bank for free (Coin Star charges a percentage). So I stopped by this Wells Fargo location for the first time and had the absolute worst experience. The security guard, the tellers, the greeter were very friendly and helpful. Unfortunately, one of the two female branch managers (the Middle Eastern? one: Marina?) was...DISGUSTING. She basically interrogated me about where I got the coins (as if I stole them?), why I'm at her branch, if this were a one time thing or if I planned to come back, and so forth. She did this in front of her staff and other customers. I was red in the face because I was so embarrassed. Then she kept telling me her vault was full and she didn't need these pennies. Then she told me that since I didn't have a merchant account, I can't exchange coins-not even rolled ones- for cash. I told her I called the main line in advance to ask if I can bring in coins and she told me that the people who answer the calls don't work in a bank so they pretty much don't know what they're talking about. I've been a Wells Fargo customer for almost 20 years now. I love Wells Fargo. Unfortunately, this woman is a poor representation of such a fine institution. I HIGHLY RECOMMEND YOU DON'T GO TO THIS BRANCH. This is the one by Vermont & Sunset.<//text>

<text>Stopped by to get my dog's allergy shot and pills for my dog and cat. No vet required. Pretty fast and easy. Covid-19 compliant.<//text><Pictures>None<//Pictures><Resp>None</Resp><GmapID>0x809b21df6c397327:0xc038cb68729fdc4<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>
<rating>1</rating>< Review>
Decide right now if your animal is just an animal or a loved one.

At 6 months we brought our puppy in wondering why he was pooping pure blood and never stopped drinking water.  We were told he ate something.   That's certainly reasonable with a pup, however the incessant water seeking was a concern with us so we had blood work done.  Results were told to us verbally that he was fine and to just limit his water consumption to an agreed amount for his weight.  They sent the lab report home with us but I didn't know what I was looking at.

My wife and daughter fell in love with this dog.  He's a companion, family member and service animal for us.  I can not overstate how much he means to this family.  The breed averages 15 years life span.

5 years later, same problem takes us to an emergency vet.  $4000 dollars later were told he's in late stage Kidney failure.  You know the one thing kidney patients need?  extra water.  You know the one thing we've limited over the years due to the dr's advice?  Water.  Doctor told us 12 ounces a day as he's a small guy.  We gave 16.

Our emergency vet cringed when we mentioned Willow rock.  This wasn't the first time he's attempted to clean up their mess.

I found the lab results that willow rock gave us 5 years ago.  I didn't know what I was looking at then, however I do now.  They overlooked the 2 single astronomically high values that indicate kidney issues.  Thanks for that Doc.

I am still trying to figure out how to tell my daughter that her best friend in the world isn't going to finish this year alive.  We expected another 10 years.

Had Willow Rock read the results that we paid for, my best friend's kidneys would probably still be limping along.  We would have gotten more than 5 years of amazingness from him.

High marks for friendly staff, clean facility and cheap meds.  Poor marks for actual doctor work.

There is nothing in this world that could make this "right" with us.  Willow rock don't bother.< /Review>

<user>101981305307935076157<//user>< text>
The stars are for the majority of the staff at willow Rock. Super kind & super sweet to me and my dog! About a year ago I took my senior dog to Dr. Carsten, he was highly recommended by my neighbors.she was suffering with arthritis i was pretty sure, and my concern was her comfort level and her ability to continue walking. At that time she was 14, with no other apparent issues. Dr Carsten was kind and certain it was arthritis, he suggested Rimadyl and i agreed to give it a try. And in the coming months it worked wonders for her! Took her in for an ear infection, they kindly squeezed us in. Several more months go by and im noticing some behaviors that caused me concern. Cries some nights and more vocal, I feared she was in pain. Get an appointment w/ dr. Carsten want him to check her out and possibly an addition to her medicine to ensure her comfort and rest. He greets us, i explain my concern about the nights she cries and is more vocal,( possibly pica )eating crazy stuff, more anxious then usual. My belief is my dog is experiencing more pain than usual. He said she was senile, i told him I wish he wouldn't say that because I'd recognize that if it were true My dog may have been old, but senile she was not. He told me he could do nothing for old age, shes getting old and what i was describing was old age and symptoms she was senile. He was done and they gave her some dumb shot that made no sense and made no improvement. No scientific proof, no suggestions, no hope, no comfort, no help for us there. I knew at that moment my dog & i were on our own & in my humble opinion dr. Carstens suggestion that my dog was senile was ignorance on his part. He could've done lab work, an xray, anything just to be certain and to give me piece of mind. That was June. I needed to get established w/ a new vet. In July, she no longer was able to keep up w/ our walking routine, she was crying in pain more and more, her leg started to swell, took her to loomis basin, she was anemic, and everything unraveled from there. July 30th we ended her pain. I am not implying my dog died because of dr. Carsten, but some blood work wouldve giving me an answer to my concern of her pain. And she certainly was in pain. Had he been thorough, he could've better prepared me for what was ahead and kept her comfortable as possible. I believe it was important for me to share my experience, and my hope is it will be helpful to someone.< /text>

<Gmap_id>0x809b21df6c397327:0xc038cb68729fdc4<//Gmap_id>< Review>
My girlfriend has taken her dogs here for almost 20 years until a recent experience. Her dog injested a sock. So we called and asked for an xray to be taken. Xray was taken and Dr. Carson advised her it was in the colon. He gave her a steroid shot and antibiotics and said it should pass, just monitor. With the miss diagnosis of this dog we admitted our dog to emergency the following day as no improvement happened, where treatment was done but overall the end result was worst case. He called us arguing that his diagnosis was correct and saying at that point he couldnt be certain, when the next vet took xrays and clearly showed us it was in the small intestine, which if he could of read the xray we would of went to emergency immediately.

Be extremely wary of Dr. Carson, as his solve all treatment is a steroid shot and antibiotics. I have taken out other dog there and EVERY time we went she was given the shot and antibiotics. Take a listen in the waiting room when other guests check out and you'll hear the same treatment for almost all animals leaving.

You get what you pay for folks. His prices are very reasonable, but you get sub par doctor service and treatment.</Review>

I was very concerned that it was purple. When I called the staff was going to get me in the next day. They were so booked. I pushed and the gal asked me to hold and told me she would go talk to the doctor. She told me to come in so that they could just run her in the back and have someone run a test. I would  to see the doctor as he was booked to the gills. When I got there the waiting room was full.I waited close to 35 to 40 mins.finally they called her back and when the test results came in I was called into a little room to speak to Dr. Kersten. I did not expect this. He came in talk to me I shirred me that my puppy was fine she did not have Parvo, She had another issue that he would treat with antibiotics. He did not have to see me or consult with me. He could've had one of his staff to do that. But he did. I have a brother who is a veterinarian out of town and I know what it's like to run that very busy business. We pet owners regarding our pets as family. < Review>
Took my Honda Fit 2015 in as the check engine line was on. Worked with Sna who is professional, polite and positive. He informed me what the wait time would be and also explained that the diagnostic would be free if I decided to do any work that was indicated via the diagnostic at their shop and $65 (way more budget friendly than any other place, Honda begins at around $200!) if I decided to go else where.
He promptly called me back in a few hours to let me know that fuel injectors needed to be replaced and suggested I call Honda to see if there had been any recall on those parts. Since there was no recall,  and that Sna gave me was reasonable, I decided to get the work done at Steve's and had everything fixed within 24 hours of taking it in!
I am really happy with the service and will be taking my car back there for an oil change soon!!< /Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
I wanted a new watch to wear at my sister's college graduation but didn't have much time to wait during a fairly quick trip to the mall.

This location made things very accessible, had a reasonably fair selection of watches considering the smaller size of the store (it's a open concept corner fixture not far from the mall's food court) and visibly alert, friendly staff.

I had an idea of what I wanted- an inexpensive watch under $500 with a sturdy band that I could wear at work or out to dinner. Luckily, the saleswoman i happened to be helped by, Anissa, was very understanding and receptive to what i would like and very accommodating to my requests and questions. Thank you Anissa!

I ended up purchasing a Citizen Eco-Drive. During the checkout process I was helped expeditiously, and offered a fairly conventional insurance plan. The staff kindly showed me how to properly adjust and care for my new watch. A man that I assume was the GM looked over his few staff with care- and while setting my watch trained his employee how to do the same in the future.

Although I often wear suits and dress nicely, I walked in wearing a local businesses T-shirt, with work pants and boots- and was treated no differently for it. This location made me feel at ease and welcomed, where other retailers felt slightly snobbish, Kevin Jewelers was approachable.

The level of product care, product knowledge, customer service and professionalism at this location was excellent.</text>

<time>1527637025667<//time><GmapID>0x80dcd9cedff677f1:0xcbe9d40ae41793a0<//GmapID><name>Anthony Broussard<//name>< review>
Went to this store for a Christmas gift and left with a beeeeeee-yoooooo-tiful ring for my gf. As a man, parting with that much money is hard, but this piece was gorgeous and the staff was super helpful in assisting me with my purchase. A small diamond ended up falling off the day after Christmas; no worries, that's what the insurance was for and I was glad I got it. Store has to send it out to get it inspected and says it going to be about 3 weeks. A month later, we get the ring back. Two days later, another stone falls off and we have to go through the same process again... and then a third time, and then a fourth. By now she's only been able to wear the ring for less than a collective week. On her fourth return visit to the store, she was informed that her ring has problems because of the necessary resize; that it is to be expected that resizing this type of ring would cause the surrounding gemstones to become unstable. My disappointment had reached a new level, knowing that I could have steered clear of this purchase and made a different selection had I been told this before, where I made it a point that the ring would need to be resized, where I was pitched that
a bonus of the insurance included unlimited size adjustments, a feature that I now know destroyed the ring. We were given the options to swap our current ring for a different one, or to keep the current one and watch as it forever falled apart. In an effort to salvage her Christmas present, we went with the first option. With their selection now barren after the holidays, we were left to select from the scraps. There was nothing close to my original selection, and she ended up picking "something" for the sake of not having nothing. I hate what we ended up with, and she thinks it's "ok", which may as well be the same feeling. While selecting the replacement, we were distracted from the price on every option presented and we're pushed by comments describing "how pretty it looked on her finger". Because of holidays sales and adjusted prices, I have no idea if what we ended up with was of a similar value or if we got ripped off. The reselection experience ended with a "well this is all we got, which do you want" kind of scenario. I've regretted this purchase for a year now and was slowly getting over my purchase until yesterday when a stone fell off the replacement ring. It was taken in today and she can expect to see it in another 3 weeks. I've purchased throw away holiday jewely before from competitor stores, that lasted until the day she got bored with them, but figured my first higher-end jewelry purchase would have led to a positive experience. I never intended on writing a review, but I just got a text from Kevin Jewlers asking for a review upon leaving the store; figured I might as well express everything I'm feeling regarding my experience. This whole endeavor has sworn me off jewelry purchases for the foreseeable future, and if I ever work up the courage to get something else, it will definitely not be from Kevin Jewelers. Leaving 1 star because I didn't actually get called a sucker by anyone while I was in the store.<//review>
